						<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>

					<div id="contentSub"><div id="mw-content-subtitle"></div></div>
					
					
					<div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content"><div class="mw-content-ltr mw-parser-output" lang="en" dir="ltr"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Professional wrestling match type</div>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1236090951">.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}@media print{body.ns-0 .mw-parser-output .hatnote{display:none!important}}</style><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This article is about the professional wrestling match. For the pay-per-view event named after this match, see <a href="/wiki/WWE_Elimination_Chamber" title="WWE Elimination Chamber">WWE Elimination Chamber</a>. For the song by Domo Genesis &amp; Alchemist, see <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(song)" class="mw-redirect" title="Elimination Chamber (song)">Elimination Chamber (song)</a>.</div>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1295905060">.mw-parser-output .infobox-subbox{padding:0;border:none;margin:-3px;width:auto;min-width:100%;font-size:100%;clear:none;float:none;background-color:transparent}.mw-parser-output .infobox-full-data:not(.notheme)>div:not(.notheme)[style]{background:#1f1f23!important;color:#f8f9fa}}@media(min-width:640px){body.skin--responsive .mw-parser-output .infobox-table{display:table!important}body.skin--responsive .mw-parser-output .infobox-table>caption{display:table-caption!important}body.skin--responsive .mw-parser-output .infobox-table>tbody{display:table-row-group}body.skin--responsive .mw-parser-output .infobox-table th,body.skin--responsive .mw-parser-output .infobox-table td{padding-left:inherit;padding-right:inherit}}</style><table class="infobox vcard"><caption class="infobox-title fn org">Elimination Chamber</caption><tbody><tr><td colspan="2" class="infobox-image logo"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Elimination_chamber_nyr06.jpg" class="mw-file-description" title="Elimination Chamber logo"><img alt="Elimination Chamber logo" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Elimination_chamber_nyr06.jpg/330px-Elimination_chamber_nyr06.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4b/Elimination_chamber_nyr06.jpg/500px-Elimination_chamber_nyr06.jpg 2x" data-file-width="528" data-file-height="400"></a></span><div class="infobox-caption">The original Elimination Chamber structure that was used between 2002 and 2015 at <a href="/wiki/New_Year%27s_Revolution_(2006)" title="New Year's Revolution (2006)">New Year's style="white-space: nowrap;">Style</th><td class="infobox-data note"><a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_match_types" title="Professional wrestling match types">6-person or more Elimination Chamber Cage Match</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label" style="white-space: nowrap;">Headquarters</th><td class="infobox-data label"><a href="/wiki/Stamford,_Connecticut" title="Stamford, Connecticut">Stamford, Connecticut</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label" style="white-space: nowrap;">Founder(s)</th><td class="infobox-data note"><a href="/wiki/Eric_Bischoff" title="Eric Bischoff">Eric Bischoff</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label" style="white-space: nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Holding_company" title="Holding company">Parent</a></th><td class="infobox-data"><a href="/wiki/WWE" title="WWE">WWE</a></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label" style="white-space: nowrap;">Website</th><td class="infobox-data"><span class="url"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://wwe.com">wwe<wbr>.com</a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>Elimination Chamber</b> is a <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling" title="Professional wrestling">professional wrestling</a> <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_match_types" title="Professional wrestling match types">elimination-based match</a> held in the <a href="/wiki/WWE" title="WWE">WWE</a>. The match was created by <a href="/wiki/Triple_H" title="Triple H">Triple H</a>, and introduced by <a href="/wiki/Eric_Bischoff" title="Eric Bischoff">Eric Bischoff</a> in November 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>1<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> It features a large <a href="/wiki/Chain-link_fencing" title="Chain-link fencing">chain-linked</a> circular <a href="/wiki/Steel" title="Steel">steel</a> structure which encloses the <a href="/wiki/Wrestling_ring" title="Wrestling ring">ring</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Description_2-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Description-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The chamber's floor is platformed over the ringside area which elevates it to ring level. Within the chamber are four inner enclosures outside each ring corner.<sup id="cite_ref-WWEMag-Design_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWEMag-Design-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> 
</p><p>Although similar in profile and nature to WWE's original large scale steel-structured match <a href="/wiki/Hell_in_a_Cell" title="Hell in a Cell">Hell in a Cell</a>, the Elimination Chamber match is a multiple-participant match wherein two participants begin the match in the ring as the remaining four are held within each inner enclosure and are released into the match at five-minute intervals (in the event of a seven-person match, three participants begin, and in the event of a tag-team match, two teams begin for a total of four participants starting). The objective is to eliminate each opponent from the match via <a href="/wiki/Pin_(professional_wrestling)" title="Pin (professional wrestling)">pinfall</a> or <a href="/wiki/Submission_(combat_sport)" class="mw-redirect" title="Submission (combat sport)">submission</a>. The winner is the last remaining participant (or team) after all others have been eliminated. As in the Hell in a Cell match, disqualifications do not apply. The original structure was 16&nbsp;ft (4.9&nbsp;m) high, 36&nbsp;ft (11&nbsp;m) in <a href="/wiki/Diameter" title="Diameter">diameter</a>, weighed over 10 short tons (9,100&nbsp;kg), and comprised 2&nbsp;mi (3.2&nbsp;km) and 6 short tons (5,400&nbsp;kg) of <a href="/wiki/Chain" title="Chain">chain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WWEMag-Design_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWEMag-Design-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ECMatch_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECMatch-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> 
</p><p>Before the establishment of the yearly <a href="/wiki/WWE_Elimination_Chamber" title="WWE Elimination Chamber">Elimination Chamber</a> <a href="/wiki/Pay-per-view" title="Pay-per-view">pay-per-view</a> (PPV) in 2010, the match was contested at other PPV events. There have been 36 Elimination Chamber matches in WWE since the concept's inception in November 2002. Every Elimination Chamber match has had a stipulation that the winner would win a championship or a future match for a championship (usually at <a href="/wiki/WrestleMania" title="WrestleMania">WrestleMania</a>, though one time the championship match occurred immediately after the Elimination Chamber match).
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc">
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="History">History</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Origin">Origin</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Origin"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Before the introduction of the Elimination Chamber match, WWE only promoted two matches in a caged environment, namely the <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_matches#Cages" class="mw-redirect" title="Professional wrestling matches">steel cage</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hell_in_a_Cell" title="Hell in a Cell">Hell in a Cell</a> matches. The steel cage was the first type of cage-based match in professional wrestling and consisted of four fenced walls of steel surrounding the <a href="/wiki/Wrestling_ring" title="Wrestling ring">ring apron</a> while the Hell in a Cell was a taller roofed version that surrounded the ring and ringside area on the ground rather than the apron. In 2002, WWE announced the creation of the Elimination Chamber, a match that combined elements of WWE's <a href="/wiki/Hell_in_a_Cell" title="Hell in a Cell">Hell in a Cell matches</a>, <a href="/wiki/Royal_Rumble#Match" title="Royal Rumble">Royal Rumble match</a>, <a href="/wiki/Survivor_Series#Survivor_Series_match" title="Survivor Series">Survivor Series match</a>, and <a href="/wiki/World_Championship_Wrestling" title="World Championship Wrestling">World Championship Wrestling</a>'s (WCW) <a href="/wiki/WarGames_match" title="WarGames match">WarGames matches</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> such as the <a href="/wiki/Countdown" title="Countdown">countdown</a> timer and time intervals from the Royal Rumble and War Games matches, the large enclosed cage format of both Hell in a Cell and WarGames and the elimination process from the Survivor Series contest and the Royal Rumble.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Brand_and_pay-per-view_designation">Brand and pay-per-view designation</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Brand and pay-per-view designation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Kane_With_A_Sidewalk_Slam.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Kane_With_A_Sidewalk_Slam.jpg/250px-Kane_With_A_Sidewalk_Slam.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="187" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Kane_With_A_Sidewalk_Slam.jpg/500px-Kane_With_A_Sidewalk_Slam.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="449"></a><figcaption>The Raw brand Elimination Chamber match at <a href="/wiki/New_Year%27s_Revolution_(2006)" title="New Year's Revolution (2006)">New Year's Revolution</a> in January 2006</figcaption></figure>
<p>To exploit additional on-screen talent after buying <a href="/wiki/World_Championship_Wrestling" title="World Championship Wrestling">World Championship Wrestling</a> (WCW) in March 2001, the following year WWE began a <a href="/wiki/WWE_brand_extension" title="WWE brand extension">brand extension</a> that divided the roster between the two brands of WWE, namely <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a> and <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Former WCW President and then Raw <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_authority_figures#General_Managers" title="Professional wrestling authority figures">General Manager</a> <a href="/wiki/Eric_Bischoff" title="Eric Bischoff">Eric Bischoff</a> formally announced the creation of the chamber during the October 21 episode of <i><a href="/wiki/WWE_Raw" title="WWE Raw">Raw</a></i> and scheduled the match to feature participants from the Raw brand roster at the <a href="/wiki/Survivor_Series_(2002)" title="Survivor Series (2002)">Survivor Series</a> in November 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The match was exclusive to the Raw brand for the first four matches and at <a href="/wiki/List_of_WWE_pay-per-view_events" class="mw-redirect" title="List of WWE pay-per-view events">joint-branded pay-per-view events</a>, but upon the creation of the <a href="/wiki/ECW_(WWE_brand)" title="ECW (WWE brand)">ECW</a> brand in 2006 the match was instead promoted for the newly created brand at <a href="/wiki/December_to_Dismember_(2006)" title="December to Dismember (2006)">December to Dismember</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-wv1_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wv1-9"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Beginning in 2008, the match became exclusive to the <a href="/wiki/WWE_No_Way_Out" title="WWE No Way Out">No Way Out</a> event and two Elimination Chamber matches were featured annually for two years among the three brands.<sup id="cite_ref-NWO08_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NWO08-10"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-NWO09_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NWO09-11"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> In 2010, WWE replaced their No Way Out event with the self-titled <a href="/wiki/WWE_Elimination_Chamber" title="WWE Elimination Chamber">Elimination Chamber</a>, a new event which continued the tradition of its predecessor. From 2008 to 2014, the match had been featured in February events only. An Elimination Chamber event took place on May 31, 2015 exclusively on the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Network" title="WWE Network">WWE Network</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> After the second brand extension in 2016, it was announced that the brands would return to having separate events. In late 2016, it was announced that Elimination Chamber would return as a <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a>-exclusive event in February 2017,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> but it switched to being <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a>-exclusive in February 2018, which was the last brand-exclusive Elimination Chamber event, as following <a href="/wiki/WrestleMania_34" title="WrestleMania 34">WrestleMania 34</a> that year, brand-exclusive pay-per-views were discontinued.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Injuries">Injuries</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Injuries"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Superplex_(Professional_wrestling_aerial_technique).jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Superplex_%28Professional_wrestling_aerial_technique%29.jpg/250px-Superplex_%28Professional_wrestling_aerial_technique%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="250" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Superplex_%28Professional_wrestling_aerial_technique%29.jpg/330px-Superplex_%28Professional_wrestling_aerial_technique%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Superplex_%28Professional_wrestling_aerial_technique%29.jpg/500px-Superplex_%28Professional_wrestling_aerial_technique%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1508" data-file-height="1885"></a><figcaption><a href="/wiki/Hardcore_Holly" title="Hardcore Holly">Hardcore Holly</a> and <a href="/wiki/CM_Punk" title="CM Punk">CM Punk</a> compete in the Extreme Elimination Chamber at <a href="/wiki/December_to_Dismember_(2006)" title="December to Dismember (2006)">December to Dismember</a> in December 2006</figcaption></figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Triple_H" title="Triple H">Triple H</a> suffered an injury during the 2002 Survivor Series match with swelling on the inside of his throat which put pressure on his <a href="/wiki/Esophagus" title="Esophagus">esophagus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vertebrate_trachea" class="mw-redirect" title="Vertebrate trachea">trachea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> This was caused after <a href="/wiki/Rob_Van_Dam" title="Rob Van Dam">Rob Van Dam</a> performed the <a href="/wiki/Professional_wrestling_aerial_techniques#Frog_splash" title="Professional wrestling aerial techniques">Five Star Frog Splash</a> off the top of one of the chambers. Triple H also expressed concern that he might have broken his wrist and noted anything could have caused it.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>16<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Sheamus" title="Sheamus">Sheamus</a> reportedly suffered a <a href="/wiki/Concussion" title="Concussion">concussion</a> during the Raw Elimination Chamber match in 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>17<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Also in 2010, <a href="/wiki/The_Undertaker" title="The Undertaker">The Undertaker</a> was involved in a pyrotechnics accident during his ring entrance. He was temporarily engulfed in flames on three occasions when the pyrotechnics were mistimed and his jacket briefly caught on fire. He suffered first and second-degree burns to his neck and chest and according to a WWE spokesperson the injury "looked like a bad sunburn". He was only allowed to participate in the match after being cleared by a ringside doctor and was given bottles of water throughout the match to douse himself with to alleviate the discomfort. Acknowledging the concern, WWE now had padded the steel floor of the chamber.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Match">Match</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Match"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Rules">Rules</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Rules"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>The Elimination Chamber match is a variation of elimination-based matches which draws elements from steel cage and Hell in a Cell matches in that the <a href="/wiki/Wrestling_ring" title="Wrestling ring">wrestling ring</a> is surrounded by a large steel-fenced cage supported by <a href="/wiki/Girder" title="Girder">girders</a>. Originally, its design was a circular-like chain-linked structure, but since 2017 it is now square and encloses the ring. Its floor is platformed over the ringside area around the ring which elevates and levels it with the ring mat. Within the Elimination Chamber, four enclosures, referred to as inner chambers or pods, are encased in <a href="/wiki/Plexiglass" class="mw-redirect" title="Plexiglass">plexiglass</a> and face the outside of each ring post.<sup id="cite_ref-Description_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Description-2"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The match is contested by six or seven participants: two or three starting in the ring, while the other four are held within each inner chamber.<sup id="cite_ref-ECMatch_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECMatch-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2018)" title="Elimination Chamber (2018)">Elimination Chamber</a> in February 2018 featured a seven-man chamber match in which three participants began. At regular intervals, one of the four participants within an inner chamber enters the match. This continues until all four have been released.  The entrance intervals are typically five minutes, though four and three minute gaps have also been used.<sup id="cite_ref-ECMatch_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECMatch-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The objective of the match is to eliminate each opponent from the match by scoring a <a href="/wiki/Pin_(professional_wrestling)" title="Pin (professional wrestling)">pinfall</a> or a <a href="/wiki/Submission_(combat_sport)" class="mw-redirect" title="Submission (combat sport)">submission</a>. These can occur in the ring or on the chamber's elevated floor, but starting with the 2010 event all pinfalls and submissions must take place within the ring. Disqualifications and count-outs do not apply in the process of elimination. The winner of the match is the last remaining participant after all others have been eliminated (or after all members of the opposing tag team are eliminated in either the tag team matches or the twelve-on-twelve tornado tag team elimination matches).<sup id="cite_ref-ECMatch_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECMatch-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The same rules apply when the match involves six tag teams, where two teams start in the ring and a new team leaves the pod and enters the ring at regular intervals.<sup id="cite_ref-ECMatch_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECMatch-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>18<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Structure">Structure</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Structure"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:WWE_Elimination_Chamber_2017.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/WWE_Elimination_Chamber_2017.jpg/250px-WWE_Elimination_Chamber_2017.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="267" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/WWE_Elimination_Chamber_2017.jpg/330px-WWE_Elimination_Chamber_2017.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/WWE_Elimination_Chamber_2017.jpg/500px-WWE_Elimination_Chamber_2017.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1944" data-file-height="2592"></a><figcaption>The new Elimination Chamber structure introduced at the <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2017)" title="Elimination Chamber (2017)">2017 event</a> and has been used every year since</figcaption></figure>
<p>According to a <i><a href="/wiki/WWE_Magazine" title="WWE Magazine">WWE Magazine</a></i> article in 2009 by WWE's <a href="/wiki/Production_designer" title="Production designer">production designer</a> Jason Robinson, who co-designed the structure, several designs for the Elimination Chamber were considered. The structure was manufactured in <a href="/wiki/Colorado_Springs,_Colorado" title="Colorado Springs, Colorado">Colorado Springs, Colorado</a> and took six to eight weeks to make from design blueprints. It cost <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US$</a> 250,000 to construct.<sup id="cite_ref-WWEMag-Design_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWEMag-Design-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The structure is made of black-painted steel with an outer structure of 16 frames, each weighing 300 pounds (140&nbsp;kg).<sup id="cite_ref-WWEMag-Design_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWEMag-Design-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The chamber is 16&nbsp;ft (4.9&nbsp;m) high and 36&nbsp;ft (11&nbsp;m) in diameter and weighs a total of 16 short tons (15,000&nbsp;kg), 10 of which consists of steel.<sup id="cite_ref-WWEMag-Design_3-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWEMag-Design-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Almanac_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Almanac-19"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ECMatch_4-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECMatch-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Each inner chamber consists of three large steel framed sheets of <a href="/wiki/Poly(methyl_methacrylate)" title="Poly(methyl methacrylate)">plexiglass</a>, costing US$225 per sheet.<sup id="cite_ref-WWEMag-Design_3-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWEMag-Design-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The chains that surround the chamber stretch 2&nbsp;mi (3.2&nbsp;km) long and weigh 6 short tons (5,400&nbsp;kg).<sup id="cite_ref-Almanac_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Almanac-19"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ECMatch_4-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECMatch-4"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>A 50&nbsp;ft (15&nbsp;m) flatbed truck is needed to transport the chamber. Assembly in the arena takes eight hours to complete and eight motors are used to suspend the structure over the ring before each event.<sup id="cite_ref-WWEMag-Design_3-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWEMag-Design-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> When not in use, the structure is stored at a dock in <a href="/wiki/Newark,_New_Jersey" title="Newark, New Jersey">Newark, New Jersey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-WWEMag-Design_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WWEMag-Design-3"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Unlike standard steel cage matches and Hell in a Cell matches, Elimination Chamber matches cannot be held at several arenas due to the structure's massive size and weight, similar to how <a href="/wiki/WarGames_match" title="WarGames match">WarGames matches</a> could only be held at certain arenas. This would play a factor in WWE dropping the annual Elimination Chamber event.<sup id="cite_ref-Steph_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Steph-20"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>In 2017, the Elimination Chamber event returned (2017's event was SmackDown-exclusive while 2018's was Raw-exclusive). In addition, the chamber structure was redesigned, becoming square instead of circular. The pods were also changed from circular to square and feature sliding doors that referees slide open from outside the chamber. At the top of the chamber at its center which is now 26&nbsp;ft (7.9&nbsp;m) tall is a large cutout of the WWE logo. The steel grates between the ring and the cage were also replaced with padding. LED lights also line the corners of the structure. The redesign was for practical purposes due to certain venues only being able to house the previous structure, allowing most venues to host the Chamber.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>21<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Variations">Variations</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Variations"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>The fifth match, held by the <a href="/wiki/ECW_(WWE_brand)" title="ECW (WWE brand)">ECW</a> brand at <a href="/wiki/December_to_Dismember_(2006)" title="December to Dismember (2006)">December to Dismember</a>, was a slight variation called the <a href="/wiki/Hardcore_wrestling" title="Hardcore wrestling">Extreme</a> Elimination Chamber.<sup id="cite_ref-ECWChamber_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECWChamber-22"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>22<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> In this variation, each chamber had one of four <a href="/wiki/Foreign_object_(professional_wrestling)" class="mw-redirect" title="Foreign object (professional wrestling)">weapons</a> for the competitors locked inside to hold on to. When each competitor's chamber opened, their weapon entered the match with them.<sup id="cite_ref-ECWeapons_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECWeapons-23"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>23<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The four weapons used in the match were a <a href="/wiki/Crowbar_(tool)" class="mw-redirect" title="Crowbar (tool)">crowbar</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Table_(furniture)#Uses" title="Table (furniture)">table</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Folding_chair#Professional_wrestling" title="Folding chair">steel folding chair</a>, and a <a href="/wiki/Barbed_wire" title="Barbed wire">barbed wire</a>-wrapped <a href="/wiki/Baseball_bat" title="Baseball bat">baseball bat</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-ECWeapons_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ECWeapons-23"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>23<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p><p>The 2015 Elimination Chamber event saw another slight variation of the match, namely the tag team chamber match. Both team members were inside of their respective pods, for a total of six tag teams in the match. Two teams, totaling four individual participants, started the match. This match was for the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Raw_Tag_Team_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="WWE Raw Tag Team Championship">WWE Tag Team Championship</a>. This variation was repeated in 2019, but for women and to determine the inaugural holders of the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Women%27s_Tag_Team_Championship" title="WWE Women's Tag Team Championship">WWE Women's Tag Team Championship</a>. Another tag team chamber match happened in 2020 for the <a href="/wiki/WWE_SmackDown_Tag_Team_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="WWE SmackDown Tag Team Championship">WWE SmackDown Tag Team Championship</a>.
</p><p>The 2018 Elimination Chamber featured the first seven-man chamber match. Due to the extra person, three competitors started the match instead of two. The 2018 event also featured the first women's chamber match, but there were no variations in the rules.
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Interference">Interference</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Interference"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>Despite the structure, interference has become common inside the Elimination Chamber. At <a href="/wiki/New_Year%27s_Revolution_(2005)" title="New Year's Revolution (2005)">New Year's Revolution</a> in January 2005, <a href="/wiki/Ric_Flair" title="Ric Flair">Ric Flair</a> distracted guest referee <a href="/wiki/Shawn_Michaels" title="Shawn Michaels">Shawn Michaels</a> allowing <a href="/wiki/Dave_Bautista" title="Dave Bautista">Batista</a> (who had been eliminated) to attack <a href="/wiki/Randy_Orton" title="Randy Orton">Randy Orton</a> so <a href="/wiki/Triple_H" title="Triple H">Triple H</a> could win the match.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>24<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> At <a href="/wiki/No_Way_Out_(2009)" title="No Way Out (2009)">No Way Out</a> in February 2009, <a href="/wiki/Edge_(wrestler)" title="Edge (wrestler)">Edge</a> attacked <a href="/wiki/Kofi_Kingston" title="Kofi Kingston">Kofi Kingston</a> during his entrance and locked himself in one of the pods becoming a participant in the match for the <a href="/wiki/World_Heavyweight_Championship_(WWE,_2002%E2%80%932013)" title="World Heavyweight Championship (WWE, 2002–2013)">World Heavyweight Championship</a> after losing the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Championship" title="WWE Championship">WWE Championship</a> earlier in the night.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>25<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> At <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2010)" title="Elimination Chamber (2010)">Elimination Chamber</a> in February 2010, <a href="/wiki/Cody_Rhodes" title="Cody Rhodes">Cody Rhodes</a> passed <a href="/wiki/Ted_DiBiase_Jr." title="Ted DiBiase Jr.">Ted DiBiase Jr.</a> a metal pipe which he used to eliminate Randy Orton in the match for the WWE Championship.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>26<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Later in the night, Shawn Michaels broke into the chamber to cost <a href="/wiki/The_Undertaker" title="The Undertaker">The Undertaker</a> his World Heavyweight Championship to <a href="/wiki/Chris_Jericho" title="Chris Jericho">Chris Jericho</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>27<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2013)" title="Elimination Chamber (2013)">Elimination Chamber</a> event in February 2013, <a href="/wiki/Mark_Henry" title="Mark Henry">Mark Henry</a> took out the remaining participants in the chamber for a World Heavyweight Championship match at <a href="/wiki/WrestleMania_29" title="WrestleMania 29">WrestleMania 29</a> after being eliminated until <a href="/wiki/WWE_SmackDown" title="WWE SmackDown">SmackDown</a> General Manager <a href="/wiki/Booker_T_(wrestler)" title="Booker T (wrestler)">Booker T</a> broke it up.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2014)" title="Elimination Chamber (2014)">Elimination Chamber</a> for the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Championship" title="WWE Championship">WWE World Heavyweight Championship</a> in February 2014, <a href="/wiki/The_Wyatt_Family" title="The Wyatt Family">The Wyatt Family</a> interfered by attacking <a href="/wiki/John_Cena" title="John Cena">John Cena</a>, leading to his eventual elimination by Randy Orton. <a href="/wiki/Kane_(wrestler)" title="Kane (wrestler)">Kane</a> would then come out to help escort The Wyatt Family out of the chamber, but would then interfere to cost <a href="/wiki/Bryan_Danielson" title="Bryan Danielson">Daniel Bryan</a> the match to Orton.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>29<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2023)" title="Elimination Chamber (2023)">Elimination Chamber</a> event in February 2023, <a href="/wiki/Logan_Paul" title="Logan Paul">Logan Paul</a> interfered by sneaking into the chamber and attacking <a href="/wiki/Seth_%22Freakin%22_Rollins" class="mw-redirect" title="Seth &quot;Freakin&quot; Rollins">Seth "Freakin" Rollins</a>, which subsequently allowed <a href="/wiki/Austin_Theory" title="Austin Theory">Austin Theory</a> to retain the <a href="/wiki/WWE_United_States_Championship" title="WWE United States Championship">WWE United States Championship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-EC2023_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EC2023-30"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Match_history">Match history</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Match history"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>The Elimination Chamber debuted at WWE's event <a href="/wiki/Survivor_Series_(2002)" title="Survivor Series (2002)">Survivor Series</a> at <a href="/wiki/Madison_Square_Garden" title="Madison Square Garden">Madison Square Garden</a> in November 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>31<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> Since the inaugural match, there have been 35 other matches (36 overall) as of <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber:_Toronto" class="mw-redirect" title="Elimination Chamber: Toronto">Elimination Chamber</a> in March 2025. The <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a> brand has been featured the most with 21 matches, including six joint-branded matches with <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a>. <a href="/wiki/ECW_(WWE_brand)" title="ECW (WWE brand)">ECW</a> has been featured in two matches, including its <a href="/wiki/No_Way_Out_(2008)" title="No Way Out (2008)">joint-branded match</a> with SmackDown. The SmackDown brand has been featured in 14 matches, including the joint-branded matches with both ECW and Raw. The <a href="/wiki/WWE_Elimination_Chamber" title="WWE Elimination Chamber">Elimination Chamber</a> event has featured more Elimination Chamber matches than any other <a href="/wiki/List_of_WWE_pay-per-view_events" class="mw-redirect" title="List of WWE pay-per-view events">WWE pay-per-view event</a>, with 27 matches being held. <a href="/wiki/Triple_H" title="Triple H">Triple H</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_Cena" title="John Cena">John Cena</a> have the most victories with 4. <a href="/wiki/Randy_Orton" title="Randy Orton">Randy Orton</a> holds the distinction of being involved in the most Elimination Chamber matches to date with 9. <a href="/wiki/Chris_Jericho" title="Chris Jericho">Chris Jericho</a> has eliminated the most wrestlers with 10.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>32<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Braun_Strowman" title="Braun Strowman">Braun Strowman</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shayna_Baszler" title="Shayna Baszler">Shayna Baszler</a> have the most eliminations in a single Elimination Chamber match (5); Baszler is also the only winner to eliminate all other opponents in a single match (Strowman's five eliminations occurred during the seven-man Chamber match).
</p><p>The majority of matches have been contested for a top-tier championship with the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Championship" title="WWE Championship">WWE Championship</a> (once as the WWE World Heavyweight Championship) being contested for the most in nine matches. The original <a href="/wiki/World_Heavyweight_Championship_(WWE,_2002%E2%80%932013)" title="World Heavyweight Championship (WWE, 2002–2013)">World Heavyweight Championship</a> was contested the second-most in seven matches, while the <a href="/wiki/ECW_World_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="ECW World Championship">ECW World Championship</a>, <a href="/wiki/WWE_Raw_Tag_Team_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="WWE Raw Tag Team Championship">WWE Tag Team Championship</a>, <a href="/wiki/WWE_SmackDown_Tag_Team_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="WWE SmackDown Tag Team Championship">SmackDown Tag Team Championship</a>, <a href="/wiki/WWE_Intercontinental_Championship" title="WWE Intercontinental Championship">Intercontinental Championship</a>, <a href="/wiki/WWE_Raw_Women%27s_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="WWE Raw Women's Championship">Raw Women's Championship</a>, and <a href="/wiki/WWE_United_States_Championship" title="WWE United States Championship">United States Championship</a> were contested in one match each. Twelve matches (two in 2008, one in 2011, 2013, 2018, 2020, 2022, and 2023, two in 2024, and two in 2025) have awarded the winners the number-one contendership for the WWE Championship, original World Heavyweight Championship, <a href="/wiki/WWE_Universal_Championship" title="WWE Universal Championship">WWE Universal Championship</a>, Raw Women's Championship, current <a href="/wiki/World_Heavyweight_Championship_(WWE)" title="World Heavyweight Championship (WWE)">World Heavyweight Championship</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Women%27s_World_Championship_(WWE)" title="Women's World Championship (WWE)">Women's World Championship</a>, respectively, at those years' <a href="/wiki/WrestleMania" title="WrestleMania">WrestleMania</a>; in 2021, SmackDown's Chamber match awarded the winner the number-one contendership for the Universal Championship that same night, which happened immediately after the Chamber match itself.
</p><p>The Elimination Chamber match has been contested only in <a href="/wiki/Indoor_arena" class="mw-redirect" title="Indoor arena">indoor arenas</a> in the United States, twice in Canada and once each in Puerto Rico and Saudi Arabia, with the 2024 event in Australia being the first to be held in an outdoor venue. From 2008 to 2014, the match had been featured in February pay-per-view events only. An Elimination Chamber pay-per-view event took place on May 31, 2015, exclusively on the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Network" title="WWE Network">WWE Network</a> and would also mark the first time the Chamber was used for a match that was not for a world championship or a future world championship match (although it would include the first ever tag team Elimination Chamber match). The <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2018)" title="Elimination Chamber (2018)">Elimination Chamber</a> in February 2018 featured the first seven-man Elimination Chamber match as well as the first Elimination Chamber match for women with the Raw Women's Championship contested. The <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2019)" title="Elimination Chamber (2019)">Elimination Chamber</a> in February 2019 featured a tag team Elimination Chamber match, the second overall tag team chamber match, but this time for women to determine the inaugural holders of the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Women%27s_Tag_Team_Championship" title="WWE Women's Tag Team Championship">WWE Women's Tag Team Championship</a>.
</p>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Compilation_release">Compilation release</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Compilation release"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<p>In July 2010, WWE released <i>Satan's Prison: The Anthology of the Elimination Chamber</i>, a DVD featuring every Elimination Chamber match as of the <a href="/wiki/Elimination_Chamber_(2010)" title="Elimination Chamber (2010)">2010 Elimination Chamber</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>70<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup> The European release of the DVD is titled <i>Iron Will</i>, primarily over the name change of the structure, match type and pay-per-view in Germany to avoid a <a href="/wiki/Brand_blunder" title="Brand blunder">brand blunder</a> with the Elimination Chamber name as it may create imagery of <a href="/wiki/Gas_chamber" title="Gas chamber">gas chambers</a> during <a href="/wiki/The_Holocaust" title="The Holocaust">The Holocaust</a> (the Elimination Chamber pay-per-view, structure and match are called No Escape in Germany).<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91"><span class="cite-bracket">[</span>71<span class="cite-bracket">]</span></a></sup>
</p>

<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Notes">Notes</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Elimination_Chamber&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Notes"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1239543626">.mw-parser-output .reflist{margin-bottom:0.5em;list-style-type:decimal}@media screen{.mw-parser-output .reflist{font-size:90%}}.mw-parser-output .reflist .references{font-size:100%;margin-bottom:0;list-style-type:inherit}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns-2{column-width:30em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns-3{column-width:25em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns{margin-top:0.3em}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns ol{margin-top:0}.mw-parser-output .reflist-columns li{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .reflist-upper-alpha{list-style-type:upper-alpha}.mw-parser-output .reflist-upper-roman{list-style-type:upper-roman}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-alpha{list-style-type:lower-alpha}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-greek{list-style-type:lower-greek}.mw-parser-output .reflist-lower-roman{list-style-type:lower-roman}</style><div class="reflist">
<div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns"><ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-Extreme_EC-41"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Extreme_EC_41-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This edition of the match was promoted as the Extreme Elimination Chamber, which featured a <a href="/wiki/Foreign_object_(professional_wrestling)" class="mw-redirect" title="Foreign object (professional wrestling)">weapon</a> in each inner chamber.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Sabu_Sub-42"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Sabu_Sub_42-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Sabu_(wrestler)" title="Sabu (wrestler)">Sabu</a> was originally scheduled to be part of the match, but due to a <a href="/wiki/Screenplay" title="Screenplay">scripted</a> attack by Hardcore Holly backstage, he was unable to take part. Holly was allowed to take his place.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Kingston_Sub-46"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Kingston_Sub_46-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Kofi_Kingston" title="Kofi Kingston">Kofi Kingston</a> was originally scheduled to be part of the match, but due to a <a href="/wiki/Screenplay" title="Screenplay">scripted</a> attack by Edge during his entrance, he was unable to take part. Edge was allowed to take his place.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Ziggler_Sub-51"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Ziggler_Sub_51-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Dolph_Ziggler" title="Dolph Ziggler">Dolph Ziggler</a> was originally scheduled to be part of the match, but was replaced by Big Show before the match due to being fired (kayfabe) on <i><a href="/wiki/WWE_SmackDown" title="WWE SmackDown">SmackDown</a></i> two days earlier.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Brand_extension-55"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-Brand_extension_55-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Brand_extension_55-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Brand_extension_55-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Brand_extension_55-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Brand_extension_55-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/WWE_brand_extension" title="WWE brand extension">brand extension</a> was not in effect from August 2011 to July 2016.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Orton_Sub-57"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Orton_Sub_57-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Randy Orton was originally scheduled to be part of the match, but due to suffering a <a href="/wiki/Screenplay" title="Screenplay">scripted</a> concussion at the hands of Daniel Bryan, he was replaced by Santino Marella, who won a battle royal to take Orton's spot.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Henry_Sub-58"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Henry_Sub_58-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Mark_Henry" title="Mark Henry">Mark Henry</a> was originally scheduled to be part of the match, but due to a <a href="/wiki/Screenplay" title="Screenplay">scripted</a> suspension by SmackDown General Manager <a href="/wiki/Theodore_Long" title="Theodore Long">Theodore Long</a>, he was replaced by The Great Khali.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-WWE_World_Heavyweight_Championship-61"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-WWE_World_Heavyweight_Championship_61-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">In December 2013, the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Championship" title="WWE Championship">WWE Championship</a> and <a href="/wiki/World_Heavyweight_Championship_(WWE,_2002%E2%80%932013)" title="World Heavyweight Championship (WWE, 2002–2013)">Word Heavyweight Championship</a> were unified to become the WWE World Heavyweight Championship, retaining the lineage of the WWE Championship while the World Heavyweight Championship was retired.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Rusev_Sub-64"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Rusev_Sub_64-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Miro_(wrestler)" title="Miro (wrestler)">Rusev</a> was originally scheduled to be part of the match, but due to suffering a broken foot, he was replaced by Mark Henry.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-WWE_Championship_name-66"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-WWE_Championship_name_66-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The WWE World Heavyweight Championship reverted to being called the WWE Championship after the reintroduction of the brand extension in 2016.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Women's_match-68"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Women's_match_68-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This was the first Elimination Chamber match to be contested between <a href="/wiki/Women_in_WWE" title="Women in WWE">female wrestlers</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-7-man_chamber-70"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-7-man_chamber_70-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This was the first Elimination Chamber to feature seven men, with three men starting the match.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Women's_Tag_Team_Titles-72"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Women's_Tag_Team_Titles_72-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">This match determined the inaugural holders of the <a href="/wiki/WWE_Women%27s_Tag_Team_Championship" title="WWE Women's Tag Team Championship">WWE Women's Tag Team Championship</a>, with three teams from <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a> and <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a> each.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Ali_Sub-74"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Ali_Sub_74-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/Mustafa_Ali_(wrestler)" class="mw-redirect" title="Mustafa Ali (wrestler)">Mustafa Ali</a> was originally scheduled to be part of the match, but due to suffering an injury, he was replaced by Kofi Kingston.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Universal_Championship_match-78"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Universal_Championship_match_78-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/WWE_Universal_Championship" title="WWE Universal Championship">WWE Universal Championship</a> match happened immediately after <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a>'s Elimination Chamber match.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Raw_Women's_Championship_WrestleMania_39-83"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Raw_Women's_Championship_WrestleMania_39_83-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Although the prize was a match for a <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a>-branded championship, the Elimination Chamber match featured three wrestlers from Raw and <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a> each.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Women's_World_Championship_WrestleMania_XL-84"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Women's_World_Championship_WrestleMania_XL_84-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Although the prize was a match for a <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a>-branded championship, the Elimination Chamber match featured wrestlers from Raw and <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-World_Heavyweight_Championship_WrestleMania_XL-86"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-World_Heavyweight_Championship_WrestleMania_XL_86-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Although the prize was a match for a <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a>-branded championship, the Elimination Chamber match featured wrestlers from Raw and <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Women's_Championship_WrestleMania_41-87"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Women's_Championship_WrestleMania_41_87-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Although the prize was a match for a <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a>-branded championship, the Elimination Chamber match featured wrestlers from Raw and <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-Undisputed_WWE_Championship_WrestleMania_41-89"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Undisputed_WWE_Championship_WrestleMania_41_89-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Although the prize was a match for a <a href="/wiki/SmackDown_(WWE_brand)" title="SmackDown (WWE brand)">SmackDown</a>-branded championship, the Elimination Chamber match featured wrestlers from <a href="/wiki/Raw_(WWE_brand)" title="Raw (WWE brand)">Raw</a> and SmackDown.</span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>
